_raw:\n    description:\n      - value(s) stored in file column\n    type: list\n    elements: str\n\"\"\"\n\nimport codecs\nimport csv\n\nfrom ansible.errors import AnsibleError, AnsibleAssertionError\nfrom ansible.parsing.splitter import parse_kv\nfrom ansible.plugins.lookup import LookupBase\nfrom ansible.module_utils.six import PY2\nfrom ansible.module_utils._text import to_bytes, to_native, to_text\nfrom ansible.module_utils.common._collections_compat import MutableSequence\n\n\nclass CSVRecoder:\n    \"\"\"\n    Iterator that reads an encoded stream and reencodes the input to UTF-8\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, f, encoding='utf-8'):\n        self.reader = codecs.getreader(encoding)(f)\n\n    def __iter__(self):\n        return self\n\n    def __next__(self):\n        return next(self.reader).encode(\"utf-8\")\n\n    next = __next__   # For Python 2\n\n\nclass CSVReader:\n    \"\"\"\n    A CSV reader which will iterate over lines in the CSV file \"f\",\n    which is encoded in the given encoding.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, f, dialect=csv.excel, encoding='utf-8', **kwds):\n        if PY2:\n            f = CSVRecoder(f, encoding)\n        else:\n            f = codecs.getreader(encoding)(f)\n\n        self.reader = csv.reader(f, dialect=dialect, **kwds)\n\n    def __next__(self):\n        row = next(self.reader)\n key, delimiter, encoding='utf-8', dflt=None, col=1):\n\n        try:\n            f = open(to_bytes(filename), 'rb')\n            creader = CSVReader(f, delimiter=to_native(delimiter), encoding=encoding)\n\n            for row in creader:\n                if len(row) and row[0] == key:\n                    return row[int(col)]\n        except Exception as e:\n            raise AnsibleError(\"csvfile: %s\" % to_native(e))\n\n        return dflt\n\n    def run(self, terms, variables=None, **kwargs):\n\n        ret = []\n\n        self.set_options(var_options=variables, direct=kwargs)\n\n        # populate options\n        paramvals = self.get_options()\n\n        for term in terms:\n            kv = parse_kv(term)\n\n            if '_raw_params' not in kv:\n                raise AnsibleError('Search key is required but was not found')\n\n            key = kv['_raw_params']\n\n            # parameters override per term using k/v\n            try:\n                for name, value in kv.items():\n                    if name == '_raw_params':\n                        continue\n                    if name not in paramvals:\n                        raise AnsibleAssertionError('%s is not a valid option' % name)\n\n                    self._deprecate_inline_kv()\n                    paramvals[name] = value\n\n            except (ValueError, AssertionError) as e:\n                raise AnsibleError(e)\n\n            # default is just placeholder for real tab\n            if paramvals['delimiter'] == 'TAB':\n AnsibleError(\"csvfile: %s\" % to_native(e))\n\n        return dflt\n\n    def run(self, terms, variables=None, **kwargs):\n\n        ret = []\n\n        self.set_options(var_options=variables, CSV (comma-separated value) format.\n        The lookup looks for the row where the first column matches keyname (which can be multiple words)\n        and returns the value in the C(col) column (default 1, which indexed from 0 means the second column in the file).\n    options:\n      col:\n        description:  column to return (0 indexed).\n        default: \"1\"\n      default:\n        description: what to return if the value is not found in the file.\n      delimiter:\n        description: field separator in the file, for a tab you can specify C(TAB) or C(\\\\t).\n        default: default: utf-8\n        version_added: \"2.1\"\n    notes:\n      - The default is for TSV files (tab delimited) not CSV (comma delimited) ... yes the name is misleading.\n      - As of version 2.11, the search parameter (text that must match the first column of the file) and filename parameter can be multi-word.\n      - For historical reasons, in the search keyname, quotes are treated\n _raw:\n    description:\n      - value(s) stored in file column\n    type: list\n    elements: str\n\"\"\"\n\nimport codecs\nimport csv\n\nfrom ansible.errors import AnsibleError, AnsibleAssertionError\nfrom ansible.parsing.splitter import parse_kv\nfrom ansible.plugins.lookup import LookupBase\nfrom ansible.module_utils.six import PY2\nfrom ansible.module_utils._text import to_bytes, to_native, to_text\nfrom ansible.module_utils.common._collections_compat import MutableSequence\n\n\nclass CSVRecoder:\n    \"\"\"\n    Iterator that reads an encoded stream and reencodes the input to UTF-8\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, f, encoding='utf-8'):\n        self.reader = codecs.getreader(encoding)(f)\n\n    def __iter__(self):\n        return self\n\n    def __next__(self):\n        return next(self.reader).encode(\"utf-8\")\n\n    next = __next__   # For Python 2\n\n\nclass CSVReader:\n    \"\"\"\n    A CSV reader which will iterate over lines in the CSV file \"f\",\n    which is encoded in the given encoding.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, f, dialect=csv.excel, encoding='utf-8', **kwds):\n        if PY2:\n            f = CSVRecoder(f, encoding=encoding)\n\n            for row in creader:\n                if len(row) and row[0] == key:\n                    return row[int(col)]\n        except Exception as e:\n            raise AnsibleError(\"csvfile: %s\" % to_native(e))\n\n        return dflt\n\n    def run(self, terms, variables=None, **kwargs):\n\n        ret = []\n\n        self.set_options(var_options=variables, direct=kwargs)\n\n        # populate options\n        paramvals = self.get_options()\n\n        for term in terms:\n            kv = parse_kv(term)\n\n            if '_raw_params' not in kv:\n AnsibleAssertionError('%s is not a valid option' % name)\n\n                    self._deprecate_inline_kv()\n                    paramvals[name] = value\n\n            except (ValueError, AssertionError) as e:\n                raise AnsibleError(e)\n\n            # default is just placeholder for real tab\n            if paramvals['delimiter'] == 'TAB':\n description: what to return if the value is not found in the file.\n      delimiter:\n        description: field separator in the file, for a tab you can specify C(TAB) or C(\\\\t).\n        default: TAB\n      file:\n        description: name of the CSV/TSV file to open.\n        default: ansible.csv\n      encoding:\n        description: Encoding (character set) of the used CSV file.\n        default: utf-8\n        version_added: \"2.1\"\n    notes:\n      - The default is for TSV files (tab delimited) not CSV (comma delimited) ... yes the name is misleading.\n      - As of version 2.11, the search parameter (text that must match the first column of the file) and filename parameter can be multi-word.\n      - For historical reasons, in the search keyname, quotes are treated\n to_bytes, to_native, to_text\nfrom ansible.module_utils.common._collections_compat import MutableSequence\n\n\nclass CSVRecoder:\n    \"\"\"\n    Iterator that reads an encoded stream and reencodes the input to UTF-8\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, f, encoding='utf-8'):\n        self.reader = codecs.getreader(encoding)(f)\n\n    def __iter__(self):\n        return self\n\n    def the input to UTF-8\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, f, encoding='utf-8'):\n        self.reader = codecs.getreader(encoding)(f)\n\n    def __iter__(self):\n        return self\n\n    def __next__(self):\n        return next(self.reader).encode(\"utf-8\")\n\n    next = __next__   # For Python 2\n\n\nclass CSVReader:\n    \"\"\"\n    A CSV reader which will iterate over lines in the CSV encoding=encoding)\n\n            for row in creader:\n                if len(row) and row[0] == key:\n                    return row[int(col)]\n        except Exception as e:\n            raise AnsibleError(\"csvfile: %s\" % to_native(e))\n\n        return dflt\n\n    def run(self, terms, variables=None, **kwargs):\n\n        ret = []\n\n        self.set_options(var_options=variables, direct=kwargs)\n\n        # populate options\n        paramvals = self.get_options()\n\n        for term in terms:\n            kv = parse_kv(term)\n\n            if '_raw_params' not in kv:\n AnsibleAssertionError('%s is not a valid option' % name)\n\n                    self._deprecate_inline_kv()\n                    paramvals[name] = value\n\n            except (ValueError,
